function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

}

if (!is_file('img/object_big.png')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: img/object_big.png');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('img/object_big.png')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): img/object_big.png');
	} else if (sha1_file('img/object_big.png') != '1e2a150b5ba29a71cc2fa7ec8486c9ffec78be4f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): img/object_big.png');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('img/object_big.png', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of img/object_big.png');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('img/object_big.png') !== '1e2a150b5ba29a71cc2fa7ec8486c9ffec78be4f') {
		if (@sha1_file('img/object_big.png') !== '4e3e0641152065df4f7895a483e7a8f6ba8cf727') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: img/object_big.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('img/object_big.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('img/object_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('img/object_big.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('img/object_big.png') !== '1e2a150b5ba29a71cc2fa7ec8486c9ffec78be4f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): img/object_big.png');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/box_texts.psd')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/objectTypes/box_texts.psd');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/box_texts.psd')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/objectTypes/box_texts.psd');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/box_texts.psd') != '58cd5af30c0d1f77078fe5b54bb0524a9614cdc7') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/box_texts.psd');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/objectTypes/box_texts.psd', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/objectTypes/box_texts.psd');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/box_texts.psd') !== '58cd5af30c0d1f77078fe5b54bb0524a9614cdc7') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/box_texts.psd') !== 'd95c5ba941290dc16c6e05fb0ac3c2bc0696784e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/objectTypes/box_texts.psd');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/objectTypes/box_texts.psd');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/objectTypes/box_texts.psd')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/objectTypes/box_texts.psd', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/box_texts.psd') !== '58cd5af30c0d1f77078fe5b54bb0524a9614cdc7') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/box_texts.psd');
		}
	}
}

// Files different: plugins/objectTypes/doi/icon_big.png

if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/icon_big.png')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/objectTypes/doi/icon_big.png');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/icon_big.png')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/objectTypes/doi/icon_big.png');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/icon_big.png') != 'b085d5e26c04b1fc6cd6b34bafa7b1c2afefeea4') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/doi/icon_big.png');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/objectTypes/doi/icon_big.png', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/objectTypes/doi/icon_big.png');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/icon_big.png') !== 'b085d5e26c04b1fc6cd6b34bafa7b1c2afefeea4') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/icon_big.png') !== 'b784f24ae6a3ea2eca270b17be8ebb4ee0e27742') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/objectTypes/doi/icon_big.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/objectTypes/doi/icon_big.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/objectTypes/doi/icon_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/objectTypes/doi/icon_big.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/icon_big.png') !== 'b085d5e26c04b1fc6cd6b34bafa7b1c2afefeea4') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/doi/icon_big.png');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/objectTypes/gs1/icon_big.png');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/gs1/icon_big.png')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/objectTypes/gs1/icon_big.png');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/gs1/icon_big.png') != '13677c9906daca193e96790b82d2145a629438cd') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/gs1/icon_big.png');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/objectTypes/gs1/icon_big.png', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/objectTypes/gs1/icon_big.png');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/gs1/icon_big.png') !== '13677c9906daca193e96790b82d2145a629438cd') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/gs1/icon_big.png') !== '700134ef8aa45428b38cf07b4e20617ec8735d6a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/objectTypes/gs1/icon_big.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/objectTypes/gs1/icon_big.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/objectTypes/gs1/icon_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/objectTypes/gs1/icon_big.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/gs1/icon_big.png') !== '13677c9906daca193e96790b82d2145a629438cd') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/gs1/icon_big.png');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big.png')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big.png');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big.png')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big.png');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big.png') != 'd754be39f7ef2dca0f37b7aa382da08664afbc4a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big.png');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big.png', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big.png');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big.png') !== 'd754be39f7ef2dca0f37b7aa382da08664afbc4a') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big.png') !== 'a783f27f690fc0b3d14de4f4b0c94db16f9f0c36') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big.png') !== 'd754be39f7ef2dca0f37b7aa382da08664afbc4a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big.png');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big__uuid.png')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big__uuid.png');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big__uuid.png')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big__uuid.png');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big__uuid.png') != '3e52f4803f0db5b2e0ec72cc79a1dadef9f1234b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big__uuid.png');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big__uuid.png', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big__uuid.png');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big__uuid.png') !== '3e52f4803f0db5b2e0ec72cc79a1dadef9f1234b') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big__uuid.png') !== '10f334520acdebe90af1bdb9de24b62e201063eb') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big__uuid.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big__uuid.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big__uuid.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big__uuid.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big__uuid.png') !== '3e52f4803f0db5b2e0ec72cc79a1dadef9f1234b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/guid/icon_big__uuid.png');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/ipv4/icon_big.png')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/objectTypes/ipv4/icon_big.png');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/ipv4/icon_big.png')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/objectTypes/ipv4/icon_big.png');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/ipv4/icon_big.png') != 'ea86a10400d568e9f1c7fda6a09eb044acb13786') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/ipv4/icon_big.png');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/objectTypes/ipv4/icon_big.png', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/objectTypes/ipv4/icon_big.png');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/ipv4/icon_big.png') !== 'ea86a10400d568e9f1c7fda6a09eb044acb13786') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/ipv4/icon_big.png') !== '0bdcbd3e4a337ee7953d25be7dfe3a0ea587b627') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/objectTypes/ipv4/icon_big.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/objectTypes/ipv4/icon_big.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/objectTypes/ipv4/icon_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/objectTypes/ipv4/icon_big.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/ipv4/icon_big.png') !== 'ea86a10400d568e9f1c7fda6a09eb044acb13786') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/ipv4/icon_big.png');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/ipv6/icon_big.png')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/objectTypes/ipv6/icon_big.png');
	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/ipv6/icon_big.png')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/objectTypes/ipv6/icon_big.png');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/ipv6/icon_big.png') != '984a060bee3b8d4b2ae199930670c570f712a5d5') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/ipv6/icon_big.png');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/objectTypes/ipv6/icon_big.png', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/objectTypes/ipv6/icon_big.png');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/ipv6/icon_big.png') !== '984a060bee3b8d4b2ae199930670c570f712a5d5') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/ipv6/icon_big.png') !== 'f82c1f47de7537e5a3e3de8ddab9ab3787467c74') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/objectTypes/ipv6/icon_big.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/objectTypes/ipv6/icon_big.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/objectTypes/ipv6/icon_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/objectTypes/ipv6/icon_big.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/ipv6/icon_big.png') !== '984a060bee3b8d4b2ae199930670c570f712a5d5') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/ipv6/icon_big.png');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/java/icon_big.png')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/objectTypes/java/icon_big.png');
	writefile_9();
	if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/java/icon_big.png')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/objectTypes/java/icon_big.png');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/java/icon_big.png') != '05e7d00e352a3059ebabe648429a18c91533f14b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/java/icon_big.png');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/objectTypes/java/icon_big.png', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/objectTypes/java/icon_big.png');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/java/icon_big.png') !== '05e7d00e352a3059ebabe648429a18c91533f14b') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/java/icon_big.png') !== 'ecfa6990f3ed698f322175c63a7506cdb41760c0') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/objectTypes/java/icon_big.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/objectTypes/java/icon_big.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/objectTypes/java/icon_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/objectTypes/java/icon_big.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/java/icon_big.png') !== '05e7d00e352a3059ebabe648429a18c91533f14b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/java/icon_big.png');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/oid/icon_big.png')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/objectTypes/oid/icon_big.png');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/oid/icon_big.png')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/objectTypes/oid/icon_big.png');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/oid/icon_big.png') != '0f24d724b4e58c3219be91d9b03a2b757bd66d59') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/oid/icon_big.png');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/objectTypes/oid/icon_big.png', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/objectTypes/oid/icon_big.png');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/oid/icon_big.png') !== '0f24d724b4e58c3219be91d9b03a2b757bd66d59') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/oid/icon_big.png') !== 'a4382480164a41eba763c41058e831240a448087') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/objectTypes/oid/icon_big.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/objectTypes/oid/icon_big.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/objectTypes/oid/icon_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/objectTypes/oid/icon_big.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/oid/icon_big.png') !== '0f24d724b4e58c3219be91d9b03a2b757bd66d59') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/oid/icon_big.png');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/other/icon_big.png')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/objectTypes/other/icon_big.png');
	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/other/icon_big.png')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/objectTypes/other/icon_big.png');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/other/icon_big.png') != '1c9129e4dc779ff4f364e9415446c61819657143') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/other/icon_big.png');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/objectTypes/other/icon_big.png', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/objectTypes/other/icon_big.png');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/other/icon_big.png') !== '1c9129e4dc779ff4f364e9415446c61819657143') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/other/icon_big.png') !== '75f9f9fdf4174cedd246ae8473ee8d1f9aa653c4') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/objectTypes/other/icon_big.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/objectTypes/other/icon_big.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/objectTypes/other/icon_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/objectTypes/other/icon_big.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/other/icon_big.png') !== '1c9129e4dc779ff4f364e9415446c61819657143') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/other/icon_big.png');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt');
	writefile_13();
	if (!is_file('whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt') != '72bdb686a7cc4cc268417955aed97419c0e9fe42') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt') !== '72bdb686a7cc4cc268417955aed97419c0e9fe42') {
		if (@sha1_file('whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt') !== '6f42dc66d765fe6aed028f58bdc2fb93ff1fb4d0') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_13();
		if (@sha1_file('whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt') !== '72bdb686a7cc4cc268417955aed97419c0e9fe42') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt');
		}
	}
}
